msg:This is the most comfortable hotel I stayed in during my visit to Henan, and it is also the best hotel in Xuchang.
It is not in the city center, so it is more convenient to drive. It was already past seven in the evening when I came out of Pangdonglai and arrived at the hotel. When checking in, the service staff brought hot tea, which was warm because it was raining. There is also a warming cabinet in the beverage area, which contains 45-degree mineral water. You can drink it as you like, which is very suitable for children, because my children feel that the water is hot and cold, and it is difficult for me to control it.
The lobby is very a**ospheric. You can go to the book bar to rest when you are tired. The book bar is also very large. The room is also very good, meeting the standards of a five-star hotel. The area is about 50 square meters, and there is a balcony with a sofa and a small table on the balcony. It is very comfortable to get up in the morning, make a cup of hot tea, and drink tea on the balcony while watching the scenery. The toilet is not electric, but a disposable toilet cover is provided, which is clean and hygienic. In addition to the regular shampoo, conditioner and shower gel, Dettol hand soap and laundry detergent are also provided, which is very friendly to children, because their clothes are too dirty every day. There is a humidifier in the room. I turned it on for a night. Henan is really dry, so I hydrated a lot. The bath water is very good and satisfactory.
This is a garden-style hotel. The environment inside the hotel is already very good. The most surprising thing is that there is a Yinmahe Park next to it. Staying in the hotel is equivalent to the back garden of the hotel. The scenery is great. Guests staying in the hotel can go for a walk by swiping their room cards. It is quite comfortable to walk and stop on rainy days.
The breakfast is great, with rich Chinese and Western food. The waiter will immediately make up for the ones that are not available. Henan's spicy soup and mutton soup are all available, and the sliced ‚Äã‚Äãnoodles and rice noodles are freshly cooked. After eating noodles for a few days, I dare not eat carbohydrates. The yogurt is freshly made. The local yogurt is quite good. The fruit is fresh. Because my throat is too dry and uncomfortable, I ate a lot of watermelon. It is a five-star recommendation for Xuchang. The main reason is that the hotel is not expensive and the price-performance ratio is first-class.

msg:I stayed for two nights and the overall feeling was good. It is suitable for vacation. Let me talk about the advantages and disadvantages in detail.
Advantages:
1. Good environment. The hotel is similar to a garden. It consists of a main building and a group of scattered villas. The greenery is great. There is also Yinmahe Park next door.
2. Good service. The staff are very warm and thoughtful, with a strong sense of service. They also humbly accept and return the suggestions.
3. The hygiene is OK. There are some small details in the room that are convenient for the people. The items that can be provided free of charge or for a fee are clearly stated on the signs, which are clear at a glance.
Disadvantages:
1. There is no refrigerator in the room, but you can ask the service to send one for temporary use. This operation is the first time I have seen it. It is surprising that such a good hotel room is not equipped with a refrigerator.
2. The floor-to-ceiling curtains are not well made. If you rest during the day, the light is very strong and dazzling, which affects your sleep.
3. The shower head is too soft, and it is not comfortable to take a bath.
4. The bathroom night light cannot be turned off manually. I don‚Äôt know if the sensor in our room is broken. It is always on, including at night, which affects sleep.
5. The location is relatively remote, and it takes about 5 kilometers to get to Pangdonglai or scenic spots. There are no supporting facilities around, few places to eat, and no shared bicycles (there are few in Xuchang, which has nothing to do with the hotel), so it is best to drive by yourself.
